    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer8961808339858680499">The <i>Peace of the Spirit Within</i> by Belzebuub takes you on a remarkable journey of self-discovery to reach the essence of peace – something that is wished for by so many and yet is so difficult to find.<br/><br/>The ancient mystics of the world wrote in sacred texts and inscribed on the walls of temples “know thyself”. Jesus said, know thyself and you shall know the depth of the all.<br/><br/>B</span>
  <span id="freeText8961808339858680499" style="display:none">The <i>Peace of the Spirit Within</i> by Belzebuub takes you on a remarkable journey of self-discovery to reach the essence of peace – something that is wished for by so many and yet is so difficult to find.<br /><br />The ancient mystics of the world wrote in sacred texts and inscribed on the walls of temples “know thyself”. Jesus said, know thyself and you shall know the depth of the all.<br /><br />Belzebuub brings the ancient esoteric techniques of self-knowledge into a modern guide for spiritual seekers who long to truly discover who they are, find peace, and their innate spiritual nature within.<br /><br />Using step-by-step exercises given by Belzebuub, learn about the origins of thoughts and emotions, how to understand the workings of the mind and subconscious, overcome negative emotions and behaviors such as anger and addictions, how to be aware in the present moment, use dreams to improve spiritually, and activate the immortal spiritual part we each have inside.<br /><br />Belzebuub presents the most practical and precise guide there is to spiritual psychology as a starter to the real inner change that leads to personal transformation and awakening, sought for and reached by mystics throughout time.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8961808339858680499" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        rated it

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer195507110" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4325446922244894393">If your goal is to get to true, lasting peace and happiness within, which practical spirituality is really all about, this is definitely the right book for you to start with. In a clear, concise and easy to understand manner, the author introduces the fundamental spiritual techniques that may serve someone as a solid base on which to build lasting peace within. Applied in daily life, these simple yet very powerful techniques may serve as the starting point of acquiring the true knowledge about o</span>
  <span id="freeText4325446922244894393" style="display:none">If your goal is to get to true, lasting peace and happiness within, which practical spirituality is really all about, this is definitely the right book for you to start with. In a clear, concise and easy to understand manner, the author introduces the fundamental spiritual techniques that may serve someone as a solid base on which to build lasting peace within. Applied in daily life, these simple yet very powerful techniques may serve as the starting point of acquiring the true knowledge about our own psychology, that of others, and the true meaning of life. On a more mundane level, this book teaches effective ways to combat negativity, depression and lower states. It explains the true nature of addictions, gambling, laziness, fears, over- and undereating and other kinds of negativity. By applying the techniques given in this book and in other books by the same author, it's possible to fundametally understand and eventually get rid of all the negativity that causes us as humans to basically live in misery, without true peace within and even without truly getting to know why we are here in the first place. Getting rid of that negativity also naturally improves our relationships with others, with ourselves and with the world around us, so in my opinion it's a very worthwhile thing to do, while we have such a great chance to do this! <br />Applying the techniques taught in this book, has really changed my life for the better, helping me to acquire more peace, happiness and overall control over my life in general, that's why I have confidence to wholeheartedly recommend this book to all those, who are also interested in a true change. <br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3546487717780375904">Ah, this book is truly a priceless gem.<br/><br/>The first time I read it though I did not quite grasp how profound it was, nor how deep I could go with the subject being taught. I wanted to understand myself better, but I did not know that I could actually change, truly change, and experience spirituality, not just read about spirituality.<br/><br/>And so the more and more I read and I dabbed into the techniques given, the more and more I realized it held the keys to self-transformation, to experience peace - the </span>
  <span id="freeText3546487717780375904" style="display:none">Ah, this book is truly a priceless gem.<br /><br />The first time I read it though I did not quite grasp how profound it was, nor how deep I could go with the subject being taught. I wanted to understand myself better, but I did not know that I could actually change, truly change, and experience spirituality, not just read about spirituality.<br /><br />And so the more and more I read and I dabbed into the techniques given, the more and more I realized it held the keys to self-transformation, to experience peace - the peace of the Spirit within.<br /><br />I've read books that contains people's experiences of what Peace is about, which while it is inspiring it does not help me much to experience that Peace. But this book just does that: it tells me how to acquire my own experience, how to reach peace within and this is truly more inspiring, and really more useful (at least to me).<br /><br />In short, this book offers the way to change, the way to ever lasting peace. It is a process, one of which I have personally greatly benefited from, so I definitely recommend this book for people interested in inner peace and the spiritual side of humanity. <br /><br />I also recommend this book if you suffer from anxiety, or deep rooted states (like depression, addictions etc..) because this book also delves into that side of our humanity and explains and teaches how to overcome these states.<br /><br />(p.s. The book is divided into 9 chapters - and it is suggested to use a week to really use the techniques taught per chapter to gain experience before moving on to the next chapter. So 9 chapters = 9 weeks. Each chapter offers guidance, techniques and has a Q&amp;A section which I found very helpful, as some of the questions I had going through the book were explained there - I followed the book as if it was a 9-week course, and I can say that I really gained a lot from it - I still go back to it though, and re-read it because it really helps my understanding). </span>
  <a data-text-id="3546487717780375904" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('oYfPvPJaeQUbrTZnWQgVVYAXA35Y/TE4vcPgIfG5/ftbLGk3odwYbeCiiIEDXdzQ5ohCGOUrfzni+uU8CTU4oQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer12588146534224670740">This account was managed by Belzebuub's publisher, but is no longer active.<br/><br/>Starting in the early 2000s, Belzebuub authored numerous books on out-of-body experiences and dreams, consciousness, and self-discovery. <br/><br/>His work was oriented around practical exercises for gaining spiritual knowledge. The practices Belzebuub explained were the ones he found most useful himself.<br/><br/>Belzebuub's last book was rel</span>
  <span id="freeText12588146534224670740" style="display:none">This account was managed by Belzebuub's publisher, but is no longer active.<br /><br />Starting in the early 2000s, Belzebuub authored numerous books on out-of-body experiences and dreams, consciousness, and self-discovery. <br /><br />His work was oriented around practical exercises for gaining spiritual knowledge. The practices Belzebuub explained were the ones he found most useful himself.<br /><br />Belzebuub's last book was released in 2010, after which he was no longer active in public life. <br /><br />BELZEBUUB’S BIOGRAPHY<br /><br />Mark (who wrote with his pen name Belzebuub) was born in the United Kingdom. As a child he had a keen interest in spiritual things, reading spiritual books from the library and creating his own esoteric ceremony at eight years old. He experienced many supernatural phenomena including ESP and poltergeist activity in his family home.<br /><br />In the early 80s he extensively studied the works of Jiddu Krishnamurti, seeing him twice in person in both 1982 and 1983 at Brockwood Park in the UK. He also read many other spiritual books and looked into other spiritual groups and traditions around this time.<br /><br />In 1990 Belzebuub stated he came across a set of spiritual practices that he found very effective, and would go on to teach.<br /><br />Belzebuub would later author online courses that proved very popular and grew to be the largest of their kind in the world at the time. These courses were run online and in person in eight countries across several continents until 2010. This course content also formed the basis of Belzebuub’s books. <br /><br />BELZEBUUB’S BOOKS AND OTHER WORKS<br /><br />Belzebuub’s work contained information on how to study oneself for inner change, use out-of-body experiences for spiritual development, and how to progress spiritually. He was able to write concisely due to his firsthand experience of the process. <br /><br />His work covered a range of topics including OBEs, near-death experiences, dreams, self-discovery, spiritual exercises, esoteric knowledge and more. Belzebuub wrote that it is the development of consciousness that enables all spiritual experience.<br /><br />Belzebuub always gave his work freely as he believed a person’s finances shouldn’t be an obstacle to receiving spiritual knowledge. Belzebuub’s books were sold through an independent publisher with no royalties ever going to him. His websites, the courses he authored, and all his videos and audio, were always free to access.<br /><br />BELZEBUUB’S MEDIA APPEARANCES<br /><br />Belzebuub was interviewed between 1997 and 2009 as an expert on out-of-body experiences and dreams internationally on TV and radio, including on the BBC and Canadian daytime TV. Belzebuub also appeared on national TV as part of a panel of experts discussing the discovery of the ancient text the Gospel of Judas.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12588146534224670740" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
</div>

<div class="clear"></div></div></div><div class="bigBoxBottom"></div></div>
